:PROPERTIES:
:TX_ID:        tx-20260703-orgasmic-1259
:TIME:         [2026-07-03 Fri 21:33:52]

:MACHINE:      Vasyls-MacBook-Pro.local
:PROJECT:      orgasmic
:TASK:         TASK-Y2ZQJ
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-daemon/src/api.rs
:REASON:       M1 MEDIUM regression (data loss): the finding-#4 atomicity fix replaced writer.mutate_file(FileMutate{transform}) — which read reviews.org INSIDE the writer flock (serialized read-modify-write) — with read-OUTSIDE-lock (std::fs::read_to_string) -> compute append_comment -> blind FileRewrite overwrite via writer.transaction. Two concurrent comment-add/consume ops on the same artifact both read the same base and the second silently clobbers the first, losing a comment or a consume. Gained atomicity, lost serialization. Fix: add a writer transactional-RMW primitive (read-under-flock + transform + tx-append committed together) and route post_artifact_feedback / post_artifact_feedback_consume through it, or guard the read->transaction window with a per-artifact mutex. Should be fixed before the artifact queue drives concurrency onto the store.
:severity:     medium
:kind:         regression
:run:          run-20260703T211936
:locations:    api.rs:9051+9095 (feedback add); api.rs:9143+9186 (consume)
:END:

:TASK:         TASK-2ZQSB
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-daemon/src/api.rs
:REASON:       M1 MEDIUM (pre-existing, surfaced by 2ZQSB): post_artifact_submit's existing-artifact read->transaction (read version/state from artifact.org, archive vN, write version+1) is NOT under the per-artifact artifact_write_lock. Two concurrent submits race on the version (lost update), and submit races regenerate's state read/flip. The Y2ZQJ M1 lock covered feedback add/consume but not submit; 2ZQSB makes it more reachable (regenerate flips state, worker submits concurrently with possible comment activity). Fix: wrap post_artifact_submit's existing-artifact read->transaction in state.artifact_write_lock(&art_dir), matching feedback/regenerate.
:severity:     medium
:kind:         concurrency
:preexisting:  true
:run:          run-20260703T233904
:END:

:REASON:       HIGH correctness: an external registration can leave an invisible permanent manager lease if supervisor bookkeeping fails after lease reservation. acquire_impl reserves (task_id, Worker) at supervisor.rs:623-638, then propagates Acquire/RunMeta session-write errors at :674-699 before inserting a RunRecord at :875-876; ManagerRegistry inserts its liveness entry only after acquire returns at manager_registration.rs:257-266. The request therefore returns 500 with neither a supervisor run nor registry entry, while manager.launch:<project> remains leased; the sweep cannot see it and the app manager keeps hitting the lease-held 500. Cancellation while acquire awaits the writer has the same gap. Fix with cancel/error-safe lease reservation cleanup in Supervisor (preferred) or an external-registration guard that releases any orphaned lease on every non-LeaseHeld failure/cancellation; add an injected session-write-failure test that proves a subsequent app manager acquire succeeds.

* TX 2026-07-15 Wed 13:13:23 reviewer.finding TASK-VKP5T
:PROPERTIES:
:TX_ID:        tx-20260715-orgasmic-1875
:TIME:         [2026-07-15 Wed 13:13:23]
:TYPE:         reviewer.finding
:ACTOR:        theaspirational@users.noreply.github.com
:MACHINE:      Vasyls-MacBook-Pro.local
:PROJECT:      orgasmic
:TASK:         TASK-VKP5T
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-daemon/src/supervisor.rs; crates/orgasmic-daemon/src/api.rs
:REASON:       MEDIUM liveness correctness: subprocess_exited treats every nonzero kill -0 result as dead and special-cases pid 0 as alive forever (supervisor.rs:2238-2248). On this host the read-only probe `id -u; ps -o pid=,uid=,sess=,comm= -p 1; /bin/kill -0 1` printed uid 501, `1 0 0 /sbin/launchd`, `Operation not permitted`, exit 1; the function therefore reports an existing EPERM process as exited and would release a live registration. Conversely POST /manager/register accepts pid=0 (api.rs:2180-2186), which bypasses TTL and can wedge the manager lease indefinitely. Fix with libc::kill(pid,0) / errno handling (ESRCH dead, EPERM alive, other errors conservative+logged), reject/normalize pid 0 to None, and test EPERM/ESRCH/zero semantics.
:severity:     medium
